### [1] [Dimensional Balance Improves Large Scale Spatiotemporal Prediction Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18793)
*Jing Chen,Shixiang Pan,Yujie Fan,Haocheng Ye,Haitao Xu,Wenqiang Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ST-Balance框架，通过空间低秩嵌入和扩展时间视野来协调时空特征表示，解决现有方法在复杂时空模式分析中的性能瓶颈问题，在交通、气象和流行病数据集上取得了显著效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时空模式分析方法存在性能瓶颈，通常只能带来增量改进且跨域迁移能力有限。作者通过空间和时间熵度量分析发现，时空复杂度不匹配越大，预测不确定性越高，尤其当模型容量固定时。这促使他们设计一个能够协调空间和时序特征表示的框架。

Method: 1) 利用空间和时间熵度量作为诊断指标，识别时空复杂度不匹配问题；2) 通过低秩矩阵嵌入压缩空间维度，保留关键结构信息；3) 扩展时间视野以捕获长程依赖关系，减少时间异质性带来的累积误差。

Result: 在城市交通、气象和流行病数据集上，该框架相比现有方法取得了显著的精度提升，并展现出广泛的应用适用性。

Conclusion: ST-Balance框架在多个时空预测任务上表现优异，具有良好跨域迁移能力，代码已开源，为更广泛的时空分析任务提供了有前景的解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate spatiotemporal pattern analysis is critical in fields such as urban traffic, meteorology, and public health monitoring. However, existing methods face performance bottlenecks, typically yielding only incremental gains and often exhibiting limited cross-domain transferability. We analyze this bottleneck through spatial and temporal entropy measures, which are used as diagnostic indicators of spatiotemporal complexity mismatch rather than as guarantees that entropy alignment alone yields better forecasting. Empirically, larger mismatch is often accompanied by higher prediction uncertainty, especially under a fixed model-capacity budget. Guided by this diagnostic, we propose a scalable, adaptive framework that harmonizes spatial and temporal feature representations. Spatial dimensionality is compressed via low-rank matrix embedding to preserve essential structure, while an extended temporal horizon captures long-range dependencies and mitigates cumulative errors arising from temporal heterogeneity. Extensive experiments on urban traffic, meteorological, and epidemic datasets demonstrate substantial accuracy gains and broad applicability across the evaluated domains, suggesting that the framework is promising for a wide range of spatiotemporal tasks beyond the current study. The code is available on GitHub at https://github.com/ST-Balance/ST-Balance.

</details>


### [2] [UCCI: Calibrated Uncertainty for Cost-Optimal LLM Cascade Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18796)
*Varun Kotte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出UCCI校准优先路由方法，通过等渗回归将标记级边际不确定性映射为查询级错误概率，并基于约束成本最小化选择升级阈值，在NER生产任务上以4B/12B LLM级联实现31%成本降低且保持F1=0.91。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM级联和模型路由方法大多使用未校准的置信度分数，且需要针对每个工作负载手动调整阈值，缺乏理论保证和自动化成本优化机制。

Method: 1) 通过等渗回归将标记级边际不确定性校准为查询级错误概率；2) 基于约束成本最小化自动选择升级阈值；3) 在三个显式假设下证明校准分数上的阈值策略是成本最优的，等渗校准的ECE样本复杂度为O(n^{-1/3})。

Result: 在75000条NER生产查询、4B/12B指令微调LLM的H100 GPU上，UCCI在微F1=0.91时降低31%推理成本（95% CI: [27%,35%]），将ECE从0.12降至0.03，优于熵阈值、分割共形路由和FrugalGPT风格阈值。

Conclusion: 校准优先的路由策略能在保持高性能的同时显著降低推理成本，且无需手动调参；所有结果基于真实模型输出和实测H100延迟而非模拟数据。

Abstract: LLM cascades and model routing promise lower inference cost by sending easy queries to a small model and escalating hard ones to a large model, but most deployed routers use uncalibrated confidence scores and require per-workload threshold tuning. We present UCCI, a calibration-first router that maps token-level margin uncertainty to a per-query error probability via isotonic regression and selects the escalation threshold by constrained cost minimization. Under three explicit assumptions, threshold policies on the calibrated score are cost-optimal, and isotonic calibration achieves O(n^{-1/3}) sample complexity for expected calibration error (ECE). On a production named entity recognition workload of 75,000 queries served by 4B and 12B instruction-tuned LLMs on H100 GPUs, UCCI cuts inference cost by 31% (95% CI: [27%, 35%]) at micro-F1 = 0.91 while reducing ECE from 0.12 to 0.03. At the same operating point, UCCI beats entropy thresholding, split-conformal routing, and a FrugalGPT-style learned threshold. All cascade results use end-to-end routing on actual model outputs and measured H100 latency, not simulated routing from global accuracies or nominal API prices.

</details>


### [3] [Simply Stabilizing the Loop via Fully Looped Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18797)
*Rao Fu,Zixuan Yang,Jiankun Zhang,Jing Ma,Hechang Chen,Yu Li,Yi Chang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出全循环Transformer（Fully Looped Transformer），通过全循环架构和注意力注入两种无参数修改，解决了循环Transformer在迭代次数增加时存在的梯度振荡和残差爆炸问题，实现了最高12次循环的稳定训练，并在下游任务上提升高达13.2%的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环Transformer虽能通过迭代复用相同模块以更少参数提升性能，但随循环次数增加出现训练不稳定性，限制了其扩展能力。

Method: 提出两种无参数修改：（1）全循环架构（Fully Looped Architecture），将跨循环信号分布到所有层以缓解残差爆炸；（2）注意力注入（Attention Injection），复用现有注意力模块抑制梯度振荡。

Result: 全循环Transformer可稳定训练至12次循环，而基线模型在此范围内崩溃；在温和场景下，下游任务平均性能提升高达13.2%。

Conclusion: 全循环Transformer提升了训练稳定性与下游性能，并可通过调整推理时的循环次数实现测试时计算资源的初步自适应平衡。

Abstract: Scaling model performance typically requires increasing model size. Looped Transformer offers a compelling alternative by iteratively reusing the same Transformer blocks, trading additional computation for improved performance without increasing parameter count or context length. Because the number of loop iterations can be adjusted at inference, it also provides a natural mechanism for balancing performance and test-time compute. However, Looped Transformer still suffers from training instability when the number of loop iterations increases. Our analysis reveals that this instability stems from two sources: gradient oscillation and residual explosion. To address these two problems, we propose the Fully Looped Transformer, which introduces two parameter-free modifications: (1) Fully Looped Architecture, which distributes inter-loop signals across all layers to mitigate residual explosion; (2) Attention Injection, which reuses the existing attention block to suppress gradient oscillation. These modifications stabilize training dynamics, enabling the Fully Looped Transformer to be trained stably up to 12 loop iterations, whereas other baseline looped models collapse in this regime. In milder settings where Looped Transformer does not collapse, Fully Looped Transformer still improves average downstream-task performance by up to 13.2\%. Overall, our experiments demonstrate that Fully Looped Transformer improves training stability, enhances downstream performance, and provides preliminary adaptability under different test-time compute budgets by varying loop iterations at inference.

</details>


### [4] [Accurate Evaluation of Quickest Changepoint Detectors via Non-parametric Survival Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18798)
*Taiki Miyagawa,Akinori F. Ebihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对快速变化检测中有限且不规则序列长度导致的ARL和ADD估计难题，本文提出基于生存分析Kaplan-Meier估计器的非参数方法KM-ARL和KM-ADD，证明了其渐近无偏性，并通过实验验证了其在实际数据集中的鲁棒性和实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ARL和ADD作为快速变化检测的核心最优性准则，在理论研究和模拟中广泛使用，但实际数据集的序列长度往往有限且不规则，导致这些指标难以直接应用。现有方法缺乏针对该场景的可靠估计手段。

Method: 将快速变化检测类比为生存分析，利用Kaplan-Meier估计器处理截断数据，从而构建ARL和ADD的非参数估计量KM-ARL和KM-ADD；推导了估计偏差界并证明其渐近无偏性（无需外推时）。

Result: 在模拟和真实数据集上，KM-ARL和KM-ADD有效增强了对有限和不规则序列长度的鲁棒性，改善了可解释性，并支持经验性模型选择。代码已开源。

Conclusion: 提出的非参数估计方法为QCD实际应用提供了可靠的性能评估工具，弥补了理论准则与真实数据场景之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: We propose non-parametric estimators for the average run length (ARL) and average detection delay (ADD) in quickest changepoint detection (QCD) under finite and irregular sequence lengths. Although ARL and ADD are widely used as optimality criteria in theoretical and simulation studies, their application to real-world datasets is hindered by limited and irregular sequence lengths. To address this issue, we propose non-parametric estimators for the ARL and ADD, termed KM-ARL and KM-ADD, by drawing an analogy between QCD and survival analysis to model detection probabilities under sequence truncation. We derive estimation bias bounds and prove that they are asymptotically unbiased unless extrapolation is required. Experiments on simulated and real-world datasets demonstrate their practical utility, enhancing robustness against limited and irregular sequence lengths, improving interpretability, and facilitating empirical, intuitive model selection. Our Python code is provided at https://github.com/TaikiMiyagawa/Kaplan-Meier-Average-Run-Length, offering ready-to-use implementations for practitioners.

</details>


### [5] [ReCrit: Transition-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Scientific Critic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18799)
*Wanghan Xu,Yuhao Zhou,Hengyuan Zhao,Shuo Li,Dianzhi Yu,Zhenfei Yin,Yaowen Hu,Fengli Xu,Wanli Ouyang,Wenlong Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ReCrit框架，将大模型与用户的批评交互建模为回合间正确性转换问题，通过强化学习奖励修正和鲁棒性、惩罚谄媚行为，并在三个科学推理基准上显著提升批评交互准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在科学推理场景中面对用户批评时，不仅会答错，还会因谄媚行为而放弃原本正确的科学答案，现有方法仅关注最终答案准确率，忽略了交互过程中正确性转换的问题。

Method: 提出ReCrit，一种转换感知的强化学习框架，将初始到批评的行为分解为修正、谄媚、鲁棒和边界四个象限，分别给予奖励或惩罚，并采用动态异步rollout与尾部自适应补全技术减少rollout等待开销。

Result: 在ChemBench、TRQA和EarthSE三个科学推理基准上，Qwen3.5-4B的平均批评准确率从38.15提升至51.49，Qwen3.5-9B从45.40提升至55.59。消融实验表明最终答案奖励几乎无收益，而转换感知奖励和象限权重能产生更可区分的训练信号。

Conclusion: ReCrit框架有效解决了科学推理中用户批评导致模型正确性下降的问题，转换感知的强化学习比最终答案奖励更适合交互场景的训练。

Abstract: Large language models can fail in critic interaction not only by answering incorrectly, but also by abandoning an initially correct scientific solution after user criticism. This is especially risky in scientific reasoning, where user criticism can turn a valid answer into an incorrect one. We frame critic interaction as an inter-turn correctness-transition problem rather than a final-answer accuracy problem, and identify three challenges: transition awareness, decoupling useful correction from harmful sycophancy, and scalable rollout. We propose ReCrit, a transition-aware reinforcement learning framework that decomposes Initial-to-Critic behavior into four quadrants: Correction, Sycophancy, Robustness, and Boundary. ReCrit rewards correction and robustness, penalizes sycophancy, and treats persistent errors as weak boundary signals. To make interaction training practical, ReCrit further uses dynamic asynchronous rollout with tail-adaptive completion to reduce rollout waiting. On three scientific reasoning benchmarks, ChemBench, TRQA, and EarthSE, ReCrit improves average Critic accuracy from 38.15 to 51.49 on Qwen3.5-4B and from 45.40 to 55.59 on Qwen3.5-9B. Ablations show that final-answer rewards provide little interaction-level gain, while transition-aware rewards and quadrant weighting produce more distinguishable training signals and larger net Critic-stage improvement. The code is available at https://github.com/black-yt/ReCrit .

</details>


### [6] [Theory-optimal Quantization Based on Flatness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18800)
*Xiusheng Huang,Zhe Li,Xuanwu Yin,Lu Wang,Yequan Wang,Dong Li,Emad Barsoum,Kang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出BDQ（双向对角量化）框架，通过优化矩阵变换来分散激活异常值分布，在LLM后训练量化中实现W4A4精度损失<1%，并在W2A4KV16极端量化下相比SOTA缩小39.1%的性能差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM后训练量化面临激活异常值导致性能严重下降的挑战，现有方法通过线性变换虽有一定缓解，但变换后的权重和激活仍存在集中分布的异常值模式，需从根本上解决异常值分布问题。

Method: 首先建模量化误差与异常值的数学关系，提出Flatness指标量化异常值分布；基于此推导出关于Flatness的理论最优解；提出BDQ框架，通过可学习的对角操作在矩阵维度间策略性地分散异常值幅度。

Result: BDQ在LLaMA-3-8B上实现W4A4量化精度下降<1%；在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B的W2A4KV16任务中，相比SOTA将性能差距缩小39.1%。

Conclusion: BDQ通过理论驱动的异常值分散策略建立了新的量化基准，有效解决了低比特量化中的异常值问题。

Abstract: Post-training quantization has emerged as a widely adopted technique for compressing and accelerating the inference of Large Language Models (LLMs). The primary challenges in LLMs quantization stem from activation outliers, which significantly degrade model performance especially at lower bit precision. While recent approaches attempt to mitigate outliers through linear transformations across feature dimensions, our analysis reveals that the transformed weights and activations still exhibit persistent outlier patterns with concentrated magnitude distributions. In this paper, we first model the mathematical relationship between quantization error and outliers, and then introduce a new metric Flatness to quantify the distribution of outliers. Based on this, we derive the theoretical optimal solution with respect to Flatness. Building on these insights, we propose Bidirectional Diagonal Quantization (BDQ), a novel post-training quantization framework that effectively disperses outlier patterns through optimized matrix transformations. BDQ strategically distributes outlier magnitudes across matrix dimensions via learned diagonal operations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that BDQ establishes a new quantization benchmark. It achieves less than 1\% accuracy drop in W4A4 quantization on the LLaMA-3-8B model. In the more challenging W2A4KV16 experiment, compared to state-of-the-art approaches, BDQ reduces the performance gap by 39.1\% on the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B model.

</details>


### [7] [PROWL: Prioritized Regret-Driven Optimization for World Model Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18803)
*Ahmet H. Güzel,Jenny Seidenschwarz,Benjamin Graham,Jonathan Sadeghi,Jeffrey Hawke,Jack Parker-Holder,Ilija Bogunovic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种KL约束对抗课程（PROWL），通过主动策略生成高误差轨迹来微调扩散世界模型，结合优先对抗轨迹缓冲区持续聚焦未解决的失败模式，从而提升视频世界模型在稀有交互关键转换上的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 被动演示数据系统性欠采样高影响交互区域，导致动作条件视频世界模型在稀有但关键的转换上不可靠，而依赖自然发生失败效率低下。

Method: 采用KL约束对抗课程训练策略暴露高误差轨迹，同时保持接近行为分布；对世界模型进行对抗微调；引入优先对抗轨迹缓冲区（PAT）基于预测误差、动作保真度和学习进度重新排序轨迹，聚焦未解决的失败模式。

Result: 在MineRL框架上，PROWL相比被动数据训练的模型提升了鲁棒性，揭示了弱行为约束下的奖励黑客行为，并证明平衡探索性失败发现与显式行为正则化至关重要。

Conclusion: 可扩展世界模型不仅受益于更大数据集，还受益于选择性生成信息丰富的训练数据；有效对抗训练需平衡探索性失败发现与行为正则化。

Abstract: Modern action-conditioned video world models achieve strong short-horizon visual realism, yet remain unreliable on rare, interaction-critical transitions that dominate downstream planning and policy performance. Because passive demonstration data systematically under-samples these high-impact regimes, improving robustness requires actively eliciting model failures rather than relying on their natural occurrence. We introduce a KL-constrained adversarial curriculum in which a policy is trained to expose high-error trajectories of a diffusion-based world model while remaining close to the behavior distribution. The world model is continuously fine-tuned on these adversarially discovered trajectories, yielding an adversarial training loop that converts rare failures into a stable, near-distribution training signal without drifting into out-of-distribution exploitation. To maintain pressure on unresolved weaknesses as the model improves, we propose a Prioritized Adversarial Trajectory (PAT) buffer that re-ranks trajectories based on prediction error, action fidelity, and learning progress, focusing training on unresolved failure modes rather than repeatedly revisiting solved cases. We implement our approach in the MineRL framework and evaluate it on held-out out-of-distribution trajectories; PROWL improves robustness over models trained on passive data alone, reveals reward-hacking behaviors under weak behavioral constraints, and demonstrates that effective adversarial world-model training critically depends on balancing exploratory failure discovery with explicit behavioral regularization. Our results suggest that scalable world models benefit not only from larger datasets, but also from selectively generating informative training data.

</details>


### [8] [Block-Based Double Decoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18807)
*Asher Labovich,Benjamin Bradley,Vanessa Alexander,Chaitanya Harsha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出基于块的双解码器（block-based double decoders）新型Transformer架构，通过双重因果块注意力掩码实现全损失监督和静态序列打包，在训练效率上媲美仅解码器模型，在推理效率上超越编码器-解码器模型，KV-cache和逐token计算量减少至少2/3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码器-解码器模型虽推理效率高，但预训练目标存在稀疏监督和动态序列长度问题，难以在大规模实践中应用。现有方法无法同时兼顾解码器-only的训练效率和编码器-解码器的推理效率。

Method: 提出块级双解码器架构，采用双重因果块注意力掩码（doubly-causal block-based attention masks），实现全损失监督训练和静态序列打包，结合了解码器-only的训练方式与编码器-解码器的推理结构。

Result: 在规模定律实验中，块级双解码器显著优于编码器-解码器，性能接近解码器-only模型；推理时KV-cache和逐token计算量减少至少2/3，且不牺牲预填充缓存或其他现有推理优化。

Conclusion: 块级双解码器有效弥合了训练效率与推理效率之间的差距，是一种可在大规模实践中替代编码器-解码器和解码器-only模型的高效架构方案。

Abstract: Encoder-decoder models offer substantial inference-time savings over decoder-only models, but their pretraining objectives suffer from sparse supervision and dynamic sequence lengths, keeping them out of practice at scale. We propose block-based double decoders, a novel transformer architecture that utilizes doubly-causal block-based attention masks to train with full loss supervision and static sequence packing, combining decoder-only training efficiency with encoder-decoder inference efficiency. In scaling law experiments, block-based double decoders strongly outperform encoder-decoders and closely track decoder-only models across scales. At inference time, they cut KV-cache memory and per-token compute by at least 2/3 without sacrificing prefill caching or other existing inference optimizations available to decoder-only models.

</details>


### [9] [Compositional Literary Primitives in Instruction-Tuned LLMs: Cross-Architectural SAE Features for Self, Style, and Affect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18808)
*Joao Paulo Cavalcante Presa,Savio Salvarino Teles de Oliveira*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过稀疏自编码器在Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct和Gemma 2 9B-IT两个指令微调大模型的中层残差流中，发现了文学原语的组合架构，包括命名门控、第一人称自我特征、风格调节器和组合情感四类特征。在27类情感分类任务中，Llama达到全覆盖，Gemma覆盖23/27，且结果非随机。跨架构不对称性体现在直接命名与间接唤起的情感表达差异上。方法上提出了三阶段验证流水线，单GPU每轮约15分钟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型内部是否存在可解释的、组合性的文学原语（literary primitives）表征，以及这些表征如何支持模型在情感分类任务中产生多样化的情感输出。

Method: 使用稀疏自编码器（SAE）对Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct和Gemma 2 9B-IT的中层残差流进行特征提取，通过logit-lens、LLM评分和5-LLM法官面板的三阶段验证流水线，在27类情感分类（Cowen-Keltner情感分类法）中评估特征组合效果。

Result: 命名门控特征、11个自我特征、风格调节器（展示而非讲述、陌生化）和组合情感特征被识别。Llama通过组合命名门控、多特征配方和单自我特征引导覆盖全部27类情感；Gemma覆盖23/27，仅"爱慕"未通过。随机判断下假阳性概率极低（约10^-3量级）。跨架构差异：Llama直接命名目标情感，Gemma通过场景意象间接唤起。

Conclusion: 大语言模型内部存在可组合的文学原语架构，情感表达可通过离散特征组合实现可解释控制。不同架构模型在情感表达策略上存在根本性差异（直接命名 vs 间接唤起），且自我特征同时承担语域标记和情感发射器的双重角色。

Abstract: We characterize a compositional architecture of literary primitives in two instruction-tuned large language models (Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct and Gemma 2 9B-IT) via sparse autoencoders on mid-depth residual streams. Four feature classes emerge: naming-gates that promote lexical tokens of a target affect, an eleven-self cluster of first-person register features, stylistic register modulators (show-don't-tell and defamiliarization), and compositional emotions that arise only from multi-feature steering. Under a forced-choice 5-LLM judge panel applied to a 27-category emotion taxonomy (Cowen-Keltner), Llama reaches full 27/27 coverage by combining naming-gates, multi-feature recipes, and single self-feature steering; Gemma reaches 23/27 with adoration as the single residual strict-fail. Under random judging, the per-cell pass probability is on the order of $10^{-3}$ and the expected number of two-seed false-positive cells across the catalog is negligible, so the observed coverage is not consistent with chance. A cross-architectural asymmetry sits in the strict-versus-soft judge contrast: on the same generations, judges agree more often on Llama outputs than on Gemma outputs because Llama outputs name the target affect more directly while Gemma outputs evoke it through scene and imagery. Both architectures contain self-features that serve simultaneously as register markers and as emotion emitters, including a single most-RLHF-loaded self-feature per architecture that intensifies the institutional Helper-AI persona at one operating regime and produces affect-categorizable output at the same calibrated coefficient. Methodologically, the paper presents a three-stage validation pipeline (logit-lens, LLM-rate, 5-LLM judge) with documented anti-patterns; the total compute is single-GPU and about 15 minutes per emotion-feature discovery cycle.

</details>


### [10] [DynaTrain: Fast Online Parallelism Switching for Elastic LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18815)
*Yuanqing Wang,Yuchen Zhang,Hao Lin,Junhao Hu,Chunyang Zhu,Quanlu Zhang,Boxun Li,Guohao Dai,Zhi Yang,Daning Cheng,Yunquan Zhang,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DynaTrain是一个分布式训练系统，通过虚拟参数空间（VPS）抽象实现了亚秒级在线重配置任意多维并行布局，在70B稠密模型和235B MoE模型上分别实现2秒和4.36秒的重配置时间，比现有方案快三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM训练具有动态性（资源波动、RLHF阶段切换、集群弹性变化），而现有训练框架基于静态执行模型构建，无法高效应对持续变化的最优并行布局需求。

Method: 提出虚拟参数空间（VPS）抽象统一所有分布式训练状态，将并行配置转化为确定性映射；在此基础上构建状态路由与传输层实现内存感知、无死锁的秩局部传输；弹性设备管理器将新世界构建与持续训练重叠以掩盖拓扑变更开销。

Result: 在高达235B参数的稠密和MoE模型上，70B稠密模型重配置时间低于2秒，235B MoE模型重配置时间4.36秒，相比基于检查点和弹性系统的方案快三个数量级，同时保持正确性。

Conclusion: DynaTrain通过VPS抽象和在线重配置机制，有效解决了动态训练环境下的并行布局优化问题，显著提升了大规模分布式训练的资源利用效率和灵活性。

Abstract: Modern large language model (LLM) training is inherently dynamic: resource fluctuations, RLHF phase shifts, and cluster elasticity continually reshape the optimal parallelism layout, posing a significant challenge to existing training frameworks built around a static execution model. We present DynaTrain, a distributed training system for sub-second, online reconfiguration across arbitrary multi-dimensional parallelism. At its core, we propose a Virtual Parameter Space (VPS) abstraction that unifies all distributed training states under one logical coordinate space, turning any parallelism configuration into a deterministic mapping and collapsing complex transition into manageable geometric intersections. On top of VPS, a state routing-and-transition layer executes rank-local transfers under a memory-aware, deadlock-free schedule, and an Elastic Device Manager overlaps new-world construction with ongoing training to mask topology-change cost. On dense and MoE models up to 235B parameters, DynaTrain reconfigures a 70B dense model in under 2s and a 235B MoE model in 4.36s, outperforming state-of-the-art checkpoint-based and elastic systems by up to three orders of magnitude while preserving correctness.

*Ahmed Šabanović,Paul Joe Maliakel,Ivona Brandić*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: INAR-VL提出了一种轻量级边缘-云路由系统，通过图像和文本复杂度信号动态分配多模态推理任务，在VQA任务上实现边缘处理36%请求、降低24%延迟、减少26%能耗，同时保持97%云端精度的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘部署VLM面临延迟与精度的权衡：云端推理精度高但存在通信延迟和能耗，边缘推理速度快但模型容量有限导致精度不足。同时图像质量和推理复杂度的异构性使得静态部署方案效果不佳。

Method: INAR-VL采用两层架构，在边缘和云端维护互补的VLM模型，利用轻量级的图像和文本复杂度信号来引导路由和模型选择，简单查询在本地执行，复杂查询则卸载到云端处理。

Abstract: Edge deployment of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) faces a tradeoff between latency and accuracy: cloud execution provides high-quality predictions but incurs communication delay and energy cost, while edge-only execution is faster but less accurate due to limited model capacity. This trade-off is further complicated by heterogeneity in image quality and reasoning complexity, making static placement suboptimal. We present INAR-VL, a lightweight edge-cloud routing system for multimodal inference in a two-tier deployment. INAR-VL maintains complementary VLMs across edge and cloud and uses lightweight image and text complexity signals to guide routing and model selection, executing simple queries locally while offloading complex ones when beneficial. Evaluation on visual question answering shows that INAR-VL executes 36% of requests on the edge, reduces latency by 24%, lowers energy by 26%, and preserves 97% of cloud-level accuracy.

### [12] [PASC: Pipeline-Aware Conformal Prediction with Joint Coverage Guarantees for Multi-Stage NLP and LLM Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18812)
*Varun Kotte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出PASC框架，通过将多阶段置信预测简化为联合最大非一致性得分的单标量共形预测问题，为NLP流水线（如NER→NED→实体类型识别、检索增强生成、智能体链路）提供有限样本、无分布假设的端到端联合覆盖保证，在三个基准上优于Bonferroni和独立CP方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NLP和LLM系统多为流水线架构（如NER→NED→实体类型识别、检索增强生成中的检索器→阅读器、智能体链路中的规划器→工具→评判器），各阶段错误会逐级累积。但现有的不确定性量化方法要么对各阶段独立校准（无法提供联合覆盖保证），要么使用Bonferroni联合界（虽能保证联合覆盖但过于保守）。需要一种既能提供联合覆盖保证又不过于保守的方法。

Method: 提出PASC（Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal）框架，将多阶段联合覆盖问题简化为一个关于联合最大非一致性得分的单标量共形预测问题。通过计算所有K个阶段中最大的非一致性分数，然后应用标准的拆分共形预测进行单次分位数计算，从而提供有限样本下无分布假设的端到端联合覆盖保证。

Result: 在CoNLL-2003的三阶段NER→NED→实体类型识别流水线上，PASC达到96.4%端到端覆盖率，优于Bonferroni的93.4%和独立CP的86.5%，且平均预测集大小完全相同（1.083）。在分布偏移到WNUT-17 Twitter和WikiNEuRal Wikipedia数据时，PASC经验性地维持了目标覆盖率，而独立CP降至59%。PASC只需单次分位数计算，运行速度比Bonferroni快1.7倍，且可扩展到K=6阶段（独立CP端到端覆盖率降至0.53）。

Conclusion: PASC提供了一种简洁高效的流水线级置信预测方法，通过降维到联合最大非一致性分数，在保持计算效率的同时实现近乎最优的联合覆盖保证，且可直接推广到复合LLM系统和智能体流水线。

Abstract: Modern NLP and LLM systems are pipelines: named entity recognition (NER) -> entity disambiguation (NED) -> entity typing, retrieval-augmented generation (retriever -> reader), and agentic chains of planner -> tool -> critic. Errors compound across stages, but existing uncertainty quantification methods either calibrate each stage independently (no joint coverage) or apply a Bonferroni union bound (joint coverage, but conservative). We present PASC (Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal), which reduces multi-stage joint coverage to a single scalar conformal prediction problem on the joint maximum nonconformity score. PASC provides a finite-sample distribution-free guarantee that all K stages are simultaneously covered with probability at least 1 - alpha, and is nearly tight up to a 1/(n+1) factor. On a three-stage NER -> NED -> entity-typing pipeline over CoNLL-2003, PASC achieves 96.4% end-to-end coverage versus 93.4% for Bonferroni and 86.5% for independent CP, at identical average prediction set size (1.083). Under distribution shift to WNUT-17 Twitter and WikiNEuRal Wikipedia data, PASC empirically maintains the target coverage in the tested shift settings while independent CP collapses to 59%. PASC requires a single quantile computation, runs 1.7x faster than Bonferroni, and scales to K = 6 stages where independent CP drops to 0.53 end-to-end coverage. The same joint-maximum-score reduction applies directly to compound LLM systems and agent pipelines.

</details>


### [13] [Composition of Memory Experts for Diffusion World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18813)
*Sebastian Stapf,Pablo Acuaviva Huertos,Aram Davtyan,Paolo Favaro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于扩散框架的世界模型，通过对比专家乘积形式集成异构记忆模型（短期记忆、长期记忆、空间长期记忆），在不增加二次成本的情况下提升时间一致性、历史回忆和导航性能，解决了现有架构中局部保真度与长期压缩之间的记忆权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型架构面临根本性记忆权衡：Transformer虽能保留局部细节但受限于二次注意力瓶颈，循环和状态空间模型虽可高效扩展但压缩历史时牺牲保真度。本文旨在克服这一权衡，将未来-过去一致性从单一架构中解耦出来。

Method: 提出扩散世界模型框架，通过对比专家乘积（contrastive product-of-experts）形式集成三个互补专家：短期记忆专家（捕获精细局部动态）、长期记忆专家（通过轻量测试时微调将情节历史存储到外部扩散权重中）、空间长期记忆专家（强制几何与空间一致性）。

Result: 在模拟和真实世界基准上，该方法在时间一致性、过去观察回忆和导航性能方面均取得改进，避免了模式坍塌，并能在不产生二次成本的情况下扩展到长上下文。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一种构建和运行记忆增强扩散世界模型的新范式，为长时序规划与决策提供了有效的记忆架构设计思路。

Abstract: World models aim to predict plausible futures consistent with past observations, a capability central to planning and decision-making in reinforcement learning. Yet, existing architectures face a fundamental memory trade-off: transformers preserve local detail but are bottlenecked by quadratic attention, while recurrent and state-space models scale more efficiently but compress history at the cost of fidelity. To overcome this trade-off, we suggest decoupling future-past consistency from any single architecture and instead leveraging a set of specialized experts. We introduce a diffusion-based framework that integrates heterogeneous memory models through a contrastive product-of-experts formulation. Our approach instantiates three complementary roles: a short-term memory expert that captures fine local dynamics, a long-term memory expert that stores episodic history in external diffusion weights via lightweight test-time finetuning, and a spatial long-term memory expert that enforces geometric and spatial coherence. This compositional design avoids mode collapse and scales to long contexts without incurring a quadratic cost. Across simulated and real-world benchmarks, our method improves temporal consistency, recall of past observations, and navigation performance, establishing a novel paradigm for building and operating memory-augmented diffusion world models.

### [14] [Symmetry in the Wild: The Role of Equivariance in Neural Fluid Surrogates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18816)
*Patryk Rygiel,Julian Suk,Kak Khee Yeung,Christoph Brune,Jelmer M. Wolterink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出AB-GATr，一个可扩展的E(3)等变神经替代模型用于CFD模拟。研究发现等变性在对称性被破坏的高度对齐数据集（如空气动力学）上可能损害分布内性能，但在几何多样的血流动力学基准中始终有益。等变性并非普遍有利，但在缺乏强数据规律性的问题中具有实际优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Anchored-Branched Geometric Algebra Transformer (AB-GATr)，一种集成了可扩展性和对称性保持的E(3)等变神经替代模型，能够高效建模耦合的表面和体积量。在汽车空气动力学和血流动力学任务上，系统比较了不同分布对齐程度下等变性的影响。

Result: 在高度对齐的空气动力学数据集中，强制等变性会降低分布内性能；在几何多样的血流动力学基准中，等变性始终有益。显式等变架构（AB-GATr）在所有基准中均优于通过数据增强隐式学习对称性的方法。

Conclusion: 等变性并非在所有领域都普遍有益，但在缺乏强数据规律性的问题中能带来实质性的优势。需要根据具体任务的数据对齐程度和对称性来权衡是否使用等变架构。

Abstract: Neural surrogates enable orders-of-magnitude acceleration of computational fluid dynamics (CFD) simulations, with the potential to transform engineering and healthcare workflows. Neural surrogate use in real-world applications requires addressing scalability to large, high-resolution surface and volume meshes, as well as to bespoke architectures, and accounting for limited training data through the use of inductive biases. Group-equivariant architectures are a principled way to introduce such bias, yet they can be detrimental when the learning problem itself breaks symmetry, for example, due to strong distributional alignment in the dataset. In this work, we investigate under which conditions equivariance improves generalization in neural CFD surrogates across tasks with increasing levels of distributional alignment and realism, covering automotive aerodynamics and blood flow (hemodynamics). To systematically assess the added value of equivariance at the limit of problem scaling, we introduce the Anchored-Branched Geometric Algebra Transformer (AB-GATr), a neural surrogate that integrates scalability and symmetry preservation to efficiently model coupled surface and volume quantities in an $E(3)$-equivariant manner. We find that on strongly aligned aerodynamics datasets, i.e., those that break symmetry, enforcing equivariance can degrade in-distribution performance. In contrast, across hemodynamic benchmarks with diverse geometries and varying alignment, equivariance is consistently beneficial. Moreover, across all benchmarks, the explicit equivariance of AB-GATr reliably outperforms implicit symmetry learning through data augmentation. Our findings showcase that equivariance is not universally beneficial across domains, yet it brings tangible advantages in problems lacking strong data regularities.

*Hongyu Gu,Jingwen Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明在Erdős-Rényi图的超位置推理任务中，梯度下降能够收敛到等权宽度优先搜索的叠加态，关键在于Möbius吸引子架构与级联监督的协同作用，并推导出无参数衰减定律精确预测实验误差。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 架构上识别了Möbius吸引子：在树形机制的S_n对称性下，层间动力学简化为1D Möbius映射，其零点集为包含等权叠加态的余维一全局最优流形。监督上提出级联监督，其反向传播同时提供选择性引导、跨层梯度持续性和逐层判别力。

Result: 端到端监督因内部梯度随(np)^{-(D-c-2)/2}衰减而无法到达最优流形；级联监督在D=3时余弦相似度实验值0.69 vs 理论预测0.71，端到端仅0.37 vs 0.35，每步误差小于0.02。

Conclusion: Möbius吸引子+级联监督=超位置推理的涌现；无参数衰减定律精确预测了不同监督策略下的收敛行为。

Abstract: Superposition allows Transformers to reason in depth, carrying an entire reasoning frontier in parallel through a bounded-depth forward pass instead of unrolling serial chain-of-thought tokens. While Zhu et al. (2025) hand-crafted an equal-weight breadth-first frontier in a single residual stream for graph reachability, it remained open whether gradient descent could ever find this target amidst permutation-symmetric saddles.
  We close this gap on Reachability-by-Superposition over Erdős-Rényi graphs by isolating architectural and supervisional contributions. Architecturally, we identify a Möbius attractor: under $S_n$-symmetry in the tree regime, layerwise dynamics reduce to a 1D Möbius map whose zero set is a codimension-one manifold of global optima containing the equal-weight superposition state.
  On the supervision side, we identify Cascade Supervision: a loss class whose backward pass simultaneously delivers (A) selectivity bootstrap, (B) gradient persistence across depth, and (C) per-step discrimination (e.g., \mathcal{L}_{sup} and \mathcal{L}_{node}). End-to-end supervision fails condition (B) and is provably insufficient: internal gradients at layer c decay as (np)^{-(D-c-2)/2} in the graph fan-out and stall before the manifold is reached.
  Our thesis: Möbius attractor + Cascade Supervision = emergence of superposition reasoning. The parameter-free decay law predicts a final-step cosine of 0.35 vs. 0.71 (end-to-end vs. cascade) at depth D=3; experiments confirm 0.37 vs. 0.69, matching within 0.02 at every step.

*Shaoke Fang,Ziang Li,Wenfei Wu,Jiatong Ji,Qingsong Liu,Ruizhi Pu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SAECache提出了一种语义自适应的前缀缓存淘汰策略，通过多队列架构、语义感知的Token权重机制和完全自适应在线学习，解决了LLM服务中不同Token类型复用率差异巨大（高达756倍）的问题，相比生产级基线实现1.4x-2.7x的TTFT提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前缀缓存淘汰策略（如LRU）将所有缓存块同等对待，忽视了LLM提示中不同Token类型（系统提示、用户查询、工具输出、模型响应、思维链推理等）复用率存在巨大差异（高达756倍）这一关键特性，导致缓存效率低下。

Method: (1) 多队列架构：将KV块路由到特定任务的队列中，采用定制化的优先级指标，捕获会话复用和结构复用两种模式；(2) 语义感知Token权重机制：通过淘汰反馈在线学习不同Token类型的复用价值；(3) 完全自适应在线学习方案：自动更新所有参数（含对数正态时序参数、位置衰减指数、队列权重和元参数），无需手动调参。

Result: 在异构工作负载下，SAECache相比生产级基线实现1.4x-2.7x的TTFT（首Token生成时间）提升。固定参数方案在工作负载不匹配时性能下降可达2.7x，而自适应方法完全避免了该问题。

Conclusion: 通过语义感知的缓存淘汰策略，可以显著提升LLM前缀缓存的效率。完全自适应的在线学习机制消除了手动调参需求，使策略能够自动适应部署环境的工作负载特征，避免因工作负载变化导致的性能退化。

Abstract: Prefix caching is a key optimization in Large Language Model (LLM) serving, reusing attention Key-Value (KV) states across requests with shared prompt prefixes to reduce expensive prefill computation. However, its benefit depends critically on the eviction policy as GPU memory is scarce, and existing policies such as LRU largely treat cached blocks uniformly. This view ignores a fundamental property of LLM prompts: not all tokens are equally worth caching. We show that different token types within a prompt, including system prompts, user queries, tool outputs, model responses, and chain-of-thought reasoning, exhibit up to 756x variation in reuse rates, yet no existing eviction policy exploits this signal. In this paper, we present SAECache (Semantic-Adaptive Eviction for prefix caches), a semantic-adaptive prefix cache eviction policy that addresses this gap through three innovations: (1) a multi-queue architecture that routes KV blocks to task-specific queues with tailored priority metrics, capturing both session reuse in multi-turn requests and structural reuse in templated single-turn requests; (2) a semantic-aware token weighting mechanism that learns the reuse value of different token types online through eviction feedback; and (3) a fully adaptive online learning schema for all parameter updates, including log-normal timing parameters, position decay power, queue weights, and meta-parameters, which eliminates manual tuning and enables automatic adaptation to deployment-specific workload characteristics. Through extensive evaluation across heterogeneous workloads, we demonstrate that SAECache achieves 1.4x-2.7x TTFT improvement over production-style baselines, while fixed-parameter alternatives can degrade by up to 2.7x under workload mismatch -- a failure mode our adaptive approach avoids entirely.

</details>


### [18] [The Routing and Filtering Structure of Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18826)
*Shafayeth Jamil,Rehan Kapadia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过分解注意力交互矩阵为路由（反对称分量）和过滤（对称分量），发现路由在低秩下运行，并提出S-D注意力解耦两者。实验表明路由会自组织成谱级联，据此可简化注意力结构，实现参数效率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准注意力机制的QK^T交互矩阵同时包含了信息路由（位置间重分配）和过滤（相关性缩放）两种耦合的计算，现有方法无法区分这两种功能，导致注意力机制的设计和优化缺乏可解释性，难以针对性地进行简化和参数压缩。

Method: 将注意力交互矩阵分解为反对称分量（路由）和对称分量（过滤）；提出S-D注意力参数化方法，通过构造保证Re(λ)≤0的稳定性，无需层归一化即可稳定训练；在5个预训练模型（1776个头）上分析路由的秩特性，并在6种规模（7M-355M）的模型上观察谱级联现象。

Result: 路由操作在低秩下运行，远低于权重核分配的路由容量；路由自组织为谱级联：首层有效秩为2，随深度扩展；前7层线性化仅导致<5%的困惑度增加，而标准注意力在此干预下崩溃；前4层替换为ELU+1线性注意力可达基线1.4%以内；级联分配的架构可减少47%-65%的注意力参数，仅增加3.9%-8.4%困惑度。

Conclusion: 路由-过滤分解使注意力的谱预算变得可读，谱级联使注意力简化变得可操作，为设计高效注意力架构提供了理论指导和实用方法。

Abstract: The attention interaction matrix $QK^{\top}$ contains two entangled computations: a skew-symmetric component that redistributes information between positions (routing) and a symmetric component that scales mutual relevance (filtering). We decompose 1776 heads across five pretrained transformers and find routing operating at low rank, well below the routing capacity allocated by the weight kernel. We introduce $S$-$D$ attention as a diagnostic parameterization that disentangles routing from filtering by construction with guaranteed stability ($\mathrm{Re}(λ) \le 0$) and trains stably without layer normalization. When disentangled and unnormalized, routing self-organizes into a spectral cascade, effective rank $2$ at the first layer, expanding with depth across six scales from 7M to 355M parameters. The cascade predicts where attention can be simplified: linearizing the first seven layers of 125M $S$-$D$ attention costs ${<}5\%$ perplexity, whereas standard attention collapses under the same intervention. The linearizable region widens with depth. Replacing the first four layers with ELU+1 linear attention reaches within $1.4\%$ of baseline at full head dimension. Cascade-allocated architectures trade attention parameters for perplexity ($47\%-65\%$ fewer attention parameters at $+3.9\%$ to $+8.4\%$ PPL). The routing-filtering decomposition makes the spectral budget legible; the cascade makes it actionable.

</details>


### [19] [Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18829)
*Zibo Diao,Jingchu Gai,Xinyue Ai,Zhang Zhang,Zhenyu He,Di He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出无损失抗蒸馏采样（LADS），通过基于查询语义内容和用户查询次数生成私有种子来控制生成过程的随机性，在不损害良性用户体验的前提下，有效防御多账户蒸馏攻击，并理论上证明其能恶化蒸馏模型的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿商业生成模型面临蒸馏攻击的严重威胁：攻击者通过收集模型生成响应来低成本训练竞争模型。现有防御方法要么牺牲良性用户的响应质量，要么依赖行为检测（易被多账户查询规避）。亟需一种能防御多账户蒸馏且不影响良性用户体验的解决方案。

Method: LADS设计了一种新型采样方案：生成过程的随机性来源于一个私有种子，该种子由查询的语义内容（映射到语义桶）和用户查询次数共同决定。良性用户每次访问获得独立采样响应；而蒸馏者的不同账户在相同语义桶内共享潜在随机性，导致收集的数据之间存在相关性。

Result: 利用均匀收敛理论证明LADS能恶化蒸馏模型在无条件生成和条件生成下的泛化差距收敛速率。在图像生成、数学推理和代码生成实验上验证了LADS能显著降低蒸馏学生模型的性能，同时保持对单个用户的精确统计保真度。

Conclusion: LADS是一种无损失的多账户蒸馏防御方法，兼顾了安全性和用户体验，为保护商业生成模型的知识产权提供了有效技术方案。

Abstract: Frontier commercial generative models face a growing threat from distillation, whereby a distiller harvests generated responses and trains a competing model of its own at drastically lower cost. Existing defenses either rely on modifying the models outputs, thereby sacrificing response quality for benign users, or on behavioral detection methods, which can be readily circumvented by distributing queries across multiple accounts. In this work, we propose Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling (LADS), a novel sampling scheme specifically designed to counter multi-account distillation while maintaining a lossless experience for benign users. Concretely, LADS derives the randomness underlying each generation from a private seed determined by the semantic content of the query and the number of times the user has queried the model. By construction, every benign user receives a response independently sampled from the original model at each visit, and thus experiences no distortion. In contrast, for a distiller, different accounts share latent randomness whenever their queries fall in the same semantic bucket. As a result, the harvested data becomes correlated, potentially reducing sample diversity and degrading generalization. Using uniform convergence theory, we show that LADS provably degrades the convergence rate of the distillers generalization gap relative to standard i.i.d. sampling in both unconditional and conditional generation settings. Experiments on image generation, mathematical reasoning, and code generation confirm that LADS substantially degrades the performance of distilled students while preserving exact statistical fidelity for individual users.

</details>


### [20] [Lying Is Just a Phase: The Hidden Alignment Transition in Language Model Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18838)
*Adil Amin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了63个基础模型中推理与真实性之间的耦合关系，发现存在一个与模型族相关的临界规模$N_c \approx 3.5$B参数，低于此规模时能力呈反相关，高于此规模时能力呈正相关。架构、数据整理和训练策略可独立改变$N_c$。研究还发现宽度归一化可消除反相关，并提出了无需模型内部信息的诊断方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然缩放定律能预测计算量与损失之间的关系，但无法解释不同能力（如推理与真实性）之间的相互作用机制。现有研究缺乏对能力间耦合关系的系统性理解，尤其缺乏对从反相关到正相关这一相变现象的分析。

Method: 对16个模型族共63个基础模型进行推理与真实性耦合分析，识别相变临界点。通过对比不同架构、数据整理和训练策略下的耦合变化，进行消融实验。采用稀疏回归ODE进行跨模型预测，并分析注意力头竞争情况。

Result: 发现临界规模$N_c \approx 3.5$B参数（95% CI: [2.9B, 13.4B]），但架构、数据整理和训练策略可独立改变$N_c$。宽度归一化可消除所有测试族中的反相关。38/40模型无竞争注意力头。ODE跨预测误差5.6%。前沿模型仍处于合作区间（r=+0.72）。

Conclusion: 能力耦合存在相变现象，模型规模并非唯一决定因素。通过架构创新、数据整理和训练策略优化可以在较小规模下实现正向耦合。提出了实用的诊断工具和干预建议，无需模型内部信息即可评估耦合状态。

Abstract: Scaling laws predict loss from compute but not how capabilities interact. We measure the coupling between reasoning and truthfulness across 63 base models from 16 families and find a regime change invisible to loss curves: below a family-dependent critical scale $N_c$, capabilities anticorrelate; above it, they cooperate. $N_c \approx 3.5$B parameters [2.9B, 13.4B] (bootstrap 95% CI), but model size is not the only variable that determines phase. Architecture, data curation, and training recipe each shift $N_c$ independently: curated training eliminated the coupling dip between Qwen generations ($0.025 \to 0.830$ at matched scale), Gemma-4 at 4B achieves coupling 0.871, characteristic of 13B+ standard-trained models, through distillation and architectural innovation, and Phi at 1B matches web-trained coupling at 10B through data curation alone. Width normalization eliminates the anticorrelation across all tested families, supporting an output-projection bottleneck. Internally, 38 of 40 models show zero competing attention heads. A sparse-regression ODE cross-predicts held-out Llama-2 at 5.6% error. The diagnostic requires no model internals -- only public benchmark scores across a model family. The cooperative regime extends to the frontier ($r = +0.72$, 34 models, 10 labs). Code, data, and an open-source activation-steering tool for any open-weight model are released alongside an interactive dashboard that diagnoses any model's coupling phase, suggests concrete interventions (data curation, width, benchmark rotation), and provides ODE scaling predictions, frontier diagnostics, and eigenstructure analysis: https://zehenlabs.com/cape/.

Method: 构建多时间步长时间序列预测框架，预测6、8、10、12、24小时后的急诊滞留时间。使用美国大学附属城市医院的真实数据，整合外部上下文数据（天气、节假日、本地大型活动）。采用DLinear和NLinear深度学习模型，并在极端拥堵场景下评估模型性能。开发了MLOps Web应用原型，集成了数据摄取、预测可视化、实验和模型重训练功能。

Abstract: Overcrowding in emergency departments (ED) remains a persistent operational challenge worldwide, causing delays in care delivery and downstream congestion. Real-world data from a university-affiliated urban hospital in the United States were utilized and integrated with external contextual data sources, including weather, holidays, and major local events. Decomposition-based Linear (DLinear) and Normalization-based Linear (NLinear) time series forecasting deep learning models showed superior performance across multiple horizons. Models were also evaluated under extreme congestion scenarios characterized by elevated boarding times. In addition, a Machine Learning Operations (MLOps) web application prototype was developed to support translation of the forecasting framework into practice through integrated data ingestion, forecast visualization, experimentation, and retraining.

### [22] [From Cumulative Constraints to Adaptive Runtime Safety Control for Nonstationary Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18841)
*Timofey Tomashevskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CPSS是一种运行时机制，通过将累积安全预算转化为自适应状态级控制约束，在持续和非平稳强化学习环境中实现每步安全决策，并在高速路合并场景中显著降低了安全违规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习中的安全性通常通过累积成本约束来保证，但这种轨迹级保证无法直接防止不安全单步决策，尤其在非平稳环境中，相同动作的风险会随上下文变化，而固定状态级阈值要么过于保守要么过于宽松。

Method: CPSS跟踪剩余安全预算，将其投影为时变可接受风险阈值，过滤预测安全成本超过该阈值的策略动作；阈值利用上下文信号在线调整，在需求高或快速变化时更严格，在预算充足时更宽松。

Result: 在非平稳高速路合并场景（highway-env）中，CPSS大幅减少了基于接近度的安全违规，增加了分离余量，且干预是选择性的而非主导学习策略。

Conclusion: 自适应的预算到阈值投影是将累积安全规范转化为有效局部安全控制的实用方法，适用于持续强化学习系统。

Abstract: Safety in reinforcement learning is often specified through cumulative cost constraints, but these trajectory-level guarantees do not directly prevent unsafe individual decisions, especially under nonstationarity. In continual and nonstationary settings, the difficulty is amplified because the risk associated with the same action can vary across contexts, while a fixed state-level threshold may be either too conservative or too weak. We propose Constraint Projection Safety Shield (CPSS), a runtime mechanism that converts a cumulative safety budget into adaptive state-level control constraints during execution. CPSS tracks the remaining safety budget, projects it into a time-varying admissible risk threshold, and filters policy actions whose predicted safety cost exceeds the active threshold. The threshold is adjusted online using contextual signals so that enforcement becomes stricter in more demanding or rapidly changing regimes and less restrictive when the available safety budget is sufficient. We analyze the resulting shielded policy and show that the mechanism guarantees per-state threshold satisfaction for executed actions, induces finite-horizon cumulative cost bounds, and yields a performance degradation bound in terms of intervention frequency and per-step reward distortion. We evaluate CPSS in nonstationary highway merging scenarios using highway-env. Across multiple seeds, CPSS substantially reduces proximity-based safety violations and increases separation margins while intervening selectively rather than dominating the learned policy. These results support adaptive budget-to-threshold projection as a practical way to transform cumulative safety specifications into effective local safety control for continual reinforcement learning systems.

### [23] [Safe Continual Reinforcement Learning under Nonstationarity via Adaptive Safety Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18842)
*Timofey Tomashevskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出LILAC+框架，通过三种自适应安全机制（基于上下文的安全约束、自适应速度约束、预算到状态的安全执行）实现非平稳环境下的安全持续强化学习，在驾驶仿真中显著减少分布偏移下的安全违规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准安全强化学习方法常假设固定约束或稳定环境条件，在分布偏移下变得不足，缺乏应对非平稳性的自适应安全机制。

Method: LILAC+框架包含三种自适应安全机制：1) 基于上下文的安全约束——利用推断和预测的环境上下文调整安全要求；2) 自适应速度约束——当环境变化速率超过智能体安全适应能力时收紧安全要求；3) 预算到状态安全执行——将累积安全要求转化为可在决策时执行的局部状态级控制约束。

Result: 在静态、已知非平稳和未知非平稳的模拟驾驶环境中，自适应安全约束相比无约束和固定约束基线，在保持竞争力任务性能的同时显著减少了分布偏移下的安全违规。

Conclusion: 安全持续强化学习需要能够响应当前状态信息、预测环境上下文、适应需求和剩余安全预算的自适应约束机制。

Abstract: Safe reinforcement learning in nonstationary environments requires safety mechanisms that adapt as environmental conditions change. Standard safe reinforcement learning methods often assume fixed constraints or stable environmental conditions, which can become inadequate under distribution shift. We propose LILAC+, a framework for safe continual reinforcement learning under nonstationarity that combines three adaptive safety mechanisms: context-based safety constraints, adaptation-speed constraints, and budget-to-state safety enforcement. Context-based constraints adjust safety requirements using inferred and predicted environmental context. Adaptation-speed constraints tighten safety requirements when the rate of environmental change exceeds the agent's ability to adapt safely. Budget-to-state enforcement converts cumulative safety requirements into local state-level control constraints that can be enforced at decision time. Together, these mechanisms provide a unified approach for proactive and reactive safety adaptation in continual reinforcement learning. We evaluate the framework in simulated driving environments under stationary, seen nonstationary, and unseen nonstationary conditions. The results show that adaptive safety constraints substantially reduce safety violations under distribution shift while maintaining competitive task performance compared with unconstrained and fixed-constraint baselines. These findings suggest that safe continual reinforcement learning requires adaptive constraint mechanisms that respond not only to current state information but also to predicted environmental context, adaptation demand, and remaining safety budget.

### [24] [TEMPO: Temporal Enforcement via Mode-Separated Policy Optimization for Trustworthy LLM Backtesting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18843)
*Zeyu Zhang,Bradly C. Stadie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TEMPO方法，通过双模式奖励和GRPO训练使大语言模型学会根据截止日期选择历史信息，避免知识泄露，在三个预测任务中将泄露率从2-13%降至0.6-3.7%，任务性能提升6-13%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在回测历史事件时，会从预训练中泄露截止日期后的知识，导致评估有效性受损。现有基于提示的方法和知识遗忘方法均无法有效解决这一问题，因为时间合规性是实例相关的。

Method: 提出TEMPO方法，包含两个核心贡献：(1) 双模式奖励机制——泄露模式将截止日期后的信息驱动至零作为硬前提，性能模式在此基础上优化任务性能；(2) 基于GRPO的训练管线，使模型发现时间有效的推理策略。

Result: 在三个预测任务和两个模型上，TEMPO将泄露率从2-13%降至0.6-3.7%，在存在强截止日期前信号的任务上，任务性能提升6-13%；在仅凭有效信息难以预测的任务上，性能得以保持。

Conclusion: 通过训练模型学会时间纪律（即根据每个实例的截止日期选择证据），而非擦除知识，可以有效解决大语言模型在时间敏感任务中的知识泄露问题，且理论证明了训练的单调收敛性和泄漏最优性。

Abstract: Backtesting large language models on historical events requires reasoning exclusively from information available before a specified cutoff date. Yet models routinely leak post-cutoff knowledge from pre-training into their reasoning, inflating apparent accuracy and undermining evaluation validity. Prompt-based constraints fail when suppressed content is causally related to the prediction, and knowledge unlearning cannot address this problem because temporal compliance is instance-specific: the same fact may be legitimate evidence for one cutoff date and a violation for another. Rather than erasing knowledge, the model must learn temporal discipline: selecting evidence conditioned on each instance's cutoff date. We propose TEMPO (Temporal Enforcement via Mode-separated Policy Optimization), which trains this discipline via two contributions: (1) a two-mode reward where a leakage mode drives post-cutoff claims to zero as a hard prerequisite before a performance mode optimizes task performance; and (2) a GRPO-based training pipeline that enables the model to discover temporally valid reasoning strategies. We prove that training monotonically decreases leakage, converges to the leak-free optimum, and improves task performance once compliance is achieved. On three prediction tasks and two models, TEMPO reduces leakage from 2~13% to 0.6~3.7% across all conditions, with task performance improving 6~13% where strong pre-cutoff signals exist and maintained where the prediction task is inherently difficult from valid information alone.

</details>


### [25] [First-Passage Prediction of Grokking Delay: ACalibrated Law under AdamW with Causal Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18845)
*Truong Xuan Khanh,Truong Quynh Hoa,Luu Duc Trung,Phan Thanh Duc*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次对AdamW优化器下的grokking延迟给出了定量预测公式 T_grok - T_mem = (1 / 2 kappa_LL eta lambda) log(V_mem / V_star)，通过校准两个参数在多种架构和任务上实现了较好的预测效果（单层Transformer MAPE 17.7%，MLP MAPE 18.0%），并提出了分位数-边际定理解释正延迟的必要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Grokking现象（模型在过拟合后突然泛化）的理论理解尚不充分，现有工作缺乏对AdamW下grokking延迟的定量预测公式，作者希望建立一个可计算的理论框架来预测延迟时间并揭示其机制。

Method: 将grokking延迟建模为首次通过时间（first-passage time），推导出延迟的封闭形式律；提出分位数-边际定理，通过参数范数分离和角度可达性两个条件建立正延迟的充要条件，并利用经验NTK特征图和验证边际分位数计算角度阈值。

Result: 在单层Transformer上26个留出运行中MAPE为17.7%（延迟范围41倍），MLP上MAPE为18.0%（N=34），跨任务扩展MAPE为23.3%（N=46, 43.5倍范围）；分位数-边际定理在模数p=97上预测角度误差仅1.3%；因果干预实验验证了范数冻结和去除权重衰减会消除grokking。

Conclusion: 首次实现了对AdamW下grokking延迟的定量预测，揭示了范数分离和角度可达性是正延迟的必要条件，但kappa_LL参数目前需经验测量而非理论推导，且方法在自然语言规模模型上的适用性尚未验证。

Abstract: We give the first quantitative prediction of grokking delay under AdamW. Treating the delay as a first-passage time, we derive a closed-form law T_grok - T_mem = (1 / 2 kappa_LL eta lambda) log(V_mem / V_star), where V_t = ||theta_t||^2 is the squared parameter norm, V_star is an architecture-dependent threshold, and kappa_LL absorbs the AdamW correction to the clean-SGD contraction rate 2 eta lambda. Calibrating (kappa_LL, V_star) on a single hyperparameter cell predicts grokking delays on 26 held-out runs with MAPE 17.7% over a 41x delay range; the law generalises to MLPs (MAPE 18.0%, N=34) and degrades to 23.3% on cross-task extension (N=46, 43.5x range), with a structured residual in which V_star / V_mem stays comparatively stable within architecture (CV about 14% on the 1L transformer).
  First-passage of V_t is necessary but not sufficient. A quantile-margin theorem establishes that positive delay requires both norm separation V_mem > V_post and angular reachability of a threshold alpha_star = arcsin(C / V_T_mem^(1/2)), where C is computable from the empirical NTK feature map and the validation-margin quantile. Calibrating C on modulus p=89 predicts alpha_star = 47.2 degrees at p=97 (observed 47.8 degrees, error 1.3%) as a prior cross-cell prediction. Causal interventions that freeze the norm or remove weight decay at memorisation eliminate grokking (0/6 vs. 3/3 baseline), trapping the angular displacement near 12 degrees.
  kappa_LL is empirically measured per architecture rather than derived from (beta_1, beta_2, epsilon); within-architecture CV stays at most 15% across four architectures, but values differ by about 2x between architectural variants beyond depth alone. Empirical scope is algorithmic tasks (modular arithmetic, sparse parity) under AdamW; whether the law transfers to natural-language scale models is open.

</details>

*Roman Kniazev,Nathanaël Fijalkow*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Transformer在序列推理任务中是否构建了任务的内部世界模型，以及该模型的结构是否反映了任务领域的结构性约束。

Method: 对8层Transformer进行机械可解释性分析，训练数据为数独求解的推理轨迹。

Result: 模型构建了子结构世界模型，信息组织围绕数独的行、列、宫（而非逐格）；在最后一层MLP中发现裸单电路，每个神经元独立检测特定单元格只剩一个可能数字并促进该数字输出。

Conclusion: 涌现世界模型的几何形状由领域的约束代数塑造而非表面呈现形式；决策电路是稀疏、单语义且完全可解释的；机械可解释性工具能够恢复Transformer解决组合推理任务的端到端算法。

Abstract: Do transformers, when trained on sequential reasoning traces, build internal models of the underlying task? And if so, does the structure of those internal representations mirror the structure of the domain? We train an 8-layer transformer on Sudoku solving traces and perform a mechanistic analysis of its internal computation. We establish two results. First, the model builds a substructure world model: it does not represent the board state cell by cell, as a human analyst would expect, but organizes information around the rows, columns, and boxes that Sudoku's constraints act on. Second, we identify a naked-single circuit: a small set of dedicated neurons in the final MLP layer, each individually detecting when exactly one digit remains possible for a specific cell, and reliably promoting that digit. These findings show that the geometry of an emergent world model is shaped by the constraint algebra of the domain, not its surface presentation, and that the resulting decision circuit is sparse, monosemantic, and fully interpretable. More broadly, they demonstrate that mechanistic interpretability tools can recover an end-to-end algorithmic account of how a transformer solves a combinatorial reasoning task.

### [27] [Exact Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18848)
*Weinuo Ou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Exact Linear Attention (ELA)，利用核函数的精确分解实现线性复杂度的Transformer注意力机制，无近似误差。通过非负性、可区分性和几何可解释性约束解决梯度爆炸和注意力稀释问题，并提出Hadamard Exp、Summation Squared Euclidean Distance和Subtraction Squared Euclidean Distance三种核函数。此外还包含Hyper Link结构、Memory Lobe模块和路由评分偏置机制三项工程创新。

Method: 1) 利用核函数精确分解实现线性复杂度注意力；2) 施加核约束保证非负性、可区分性和几何可解释性；3) 提出三种核函数（Hadamard Exp Kernel、Summation Squared Euclidean Distance Kernel、Subtraction Squared Euclidean Distance Kernel）；4) 设计Hyper Link结构替代残差连接缓解梯度退化；5) 提出Memory Lobe模块实现跨层变换流捕获和隐式强化学习；6) 引入路由评分偏置机制提升MoE可解释性和语义对齐。

Conclusion: ELA通过精确核分解从根本上解决了线性注意力的精度与稳定性问题，三类工程创新进一步增强了模型的可训练性、记忆机制和可解释性，为高效Transformer架构提供了新范式。

Abstract: This paper introduces Exact Linear Attention (ELA), a mechanism that achieves linear computational complexity for Transformer attention by leveraging the exact decomposition property of kernel functions, without any approximation error. It identifies and addresses gradient explosion and token attention dilution in prior linear attention methods by imposing kernel constraints that ensure non-negativity, discriminability, and geometric interpretability. Several kernel functions are proposed, including the Hadamard Exp Kernel, Summation Squared Euclidean Distance Kernel, and Subtraction Squared Euclidean Distance Kernel. Beyond the core attention formulation, the paper presents three engineering innovations: a Hyper Link structure that replaces traditional residual connections to mitigate gradient degradation, a Memory Lobe module based on bidirectional linear attention that captures transformation flow across layers to implement qualitative memory and an implicit reinforcement learning paradigm, and a routing score based bias mechanism for Mixture of Experts to improve interpretability and semantic alignment.

While current methods focus on local explanations, INSIGHTS generates sample summaries that offer a comprehensive overview of model behavior. We evaluate INSIGHTS through experiments, interviews, and a user study. Our results indicate INSIGHTS effectively constructs comprehensive, diverse time series subsets, producing summaries manageable for individual evaluation. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Family-FL三层架构：以家庭为自然隐私边界，在全局同步前进行族内聚合；设计硬件约束下的Tiny CNN-LSTM架构（669参数），经INT8量化后仅占4.65KB Flash和2.95KB RAM，适配STC32G12K128类微控制器。

We propose Family-Grouped Hierarchical Federated Learning (Family-FL), a three-tier architecture that uses the family as a natural privacy boundary for intra-family aggregation before global synchronization. We further design a hardware-constrained Tiny CNN-LSTM architecture with only 669 parameters, INT8-quantized to occupy merely 4.65KB Flash and 2.95KB RAM, meeting the constraints of STC32G12K128-class microcontrollers. Experiments on the MIT-BIH Arrhythmia Database (mean of 5 independent runs with different seeds) demonstrate that Family-FL reduces communication volume by 76.7% compared to FedAvg while maintaining comparable accuracy. Family-FL-Tiny achieves 91.9 +/- 1.2% accuracy with macro-F1 of 0.483 +/- 0.031, reducing total communication to 0.31% of FedAvg. The model achieves reliable ventricular arrhythmia detection (per-class F1 = 0.80), the most clinically critical abnormality for home-based preliminary screening. These results demonstrate the technical feasibility of privacy-preserving federated learning on ultra-resource-constrained microcontrollers through simulation-based evaluation. We honestly discuss limitations: no hardware deployment, single-dataset validation (MIT-BIH, 47 subjects), reduced rare-class sensitivity, and absence of formal differential privacy guarantees.

### [30] [SAGE: Shaping Anchors for Guided Exploration in RLVR of LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18864)
*Chanuk Lee,Minki Kang,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出RLVR在推理任务中提升pass@1但难以提升pass@k的根本原因是reverse-KL正则化将策略锚定在参考分布上，抑制了多样化推理模式的涌现。作者提出SAGE框架，通过引导函数重塑reverse-KL的锚定分布来实现可控的经验支持集扩展，从而同时提升pass@1和pass@k。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究RLVR为何能提升pass@1却难以提升pass@k，质疑其是否真正赋予模型新的推理能力，并分析其中的结构性约束。

Method: 提出SAGE框架，通过设计一个引导函数q(x,y)来重塑reverse-KL正则化中的锚定分布，而非简单移除或替换KL项，从而实现可控的经验支持集扩展。

Result: 在多个具有挑战性的数学推理基准上，SAGE在pass@1和pass@k上均取得了一致的改进。

Conclusion: reverse-KL正则化是限制推理模式多样性的关键结构性约束；简单移除或替换为forward-KL均会破坏效率-覆盖权衡；SAGE通过重塑锚定分布有效解决了这一矛盾。

Abstract: Recent studies observe that reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) reliably improves pass@1 on reasoning tasks, yet often fails to yield comparable gains in pass@k, raising the question of whether RLVR genuinely enables large language models to acquire novel reasoning abilities or merely enhances the efficiency of sampling reasoning modes already present in the base model. Prior analyses largely support the latter view, attributing this limitation to structural properties of standard RLVR objectives that result in insufficient exploration pressure. In this work, we argue that a central structural constraint arises from reverse-KL regularization, which stabilizes training but inherently anchors the policy to the reference distribution, thereby suppressing the emergence of alternative reasoning modes. However, we show that neither removing the KL term nor replacing it with forward-KL provides a satisfactory solution, as both disrupt the efficiency-coverage trade-off by either inducing reward hacking or allocating probability mass to off-target regions. To resolve this tension, we propose SAGE, a principled framework that enables controllable empirical support expansion by reshaping the reverse-KL anchor distribution itself through a guide function q(x,y), achieving consistent improvements in both pass@1 and pass@k across challenging mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Our code is available at https://github.com/tally0818/SAGE.

Abstract: Self-attention serves as the core foundation of large-scale transformer pretraining, but its quadratic token interaction cost makes inference expensive. This paper revisits attention replacement through the lens of sparsity. Based on the observation of diverse sparsity patterns across transformer layers, we posit that pretrained transformers decompose the complex token dependency across tokens into various sequence-to-sequence mappings of diverse complexities, where some layer functionalities can be approximated and replaced with much simpler sequential modules without loss. We evaluate this premise using a plug-and-play layer-wise distillation framework to approximate and replace attention functionalities in pretrained vision transformer models. Controlled group-wise replacements under a fixed training budget reveal a clear pattern: substituting layers with sparser attention incurs substantially smaller accuracy drops than replacing denser ones. We further impose explicit attention sparsity on the pretrained ViT via AViT-style token retention and perform sparsity-guided distillation for sequential replacing models, where we see increasing teacher sparsity consistently reduces the student-teacher gap. The proposed method achieves efficient attention replacement for reduced parameter size and latency through the guidance of attention sparsity.

Abstract: Reconstructing continuous flow fields from sparse surface-mounted sensors is central to aerodynamic design, flow control, and digital-twin instrumentation. Existing neural methods for this task typically encode sensor readings into implicit latent codes with little spatial interpretability and limited formal guidance on how representational capacity should scale with observation count. Inspired by 3D Gaussian Splatting, we introduce FLUIDSPLAT, a sensor-conditioned model that predicts K anisotropic Gaussian primitives forming a partition-of-unity scaffold, a spatially explicit and interpretable intermediate representation of the flow. For an idealized Gaussian primitive estimator, we prove an $O(K^{-s/d})$ approximation rate for fields with Sobolev smoothness $s$; incorporating $N$ noisy observations yields a squared-risk decomposition with bias $O(K^{-2s/d})$ and variance $O(σ^{2}K/N)$.Balancing the two yields $K^{*}\!\sim\!(N/σ^{2})^{d/(2s+d)}$: primitive count cannot grow freely under sparse sensing, revealing a variance bottleneck that motivates complementing the scaffold with a state-conditioned residual decoder. Motivation: 现有自动提示优化方法仅关注性能，忽略推理成本或延迟等竞争目标；现有多目标优化工作直接使用现成的NSGA-II，忽视了优化效率。

Method: 提出MO-CAPO算法，联合优化性能与推理成本，引入预算分配机制提升优化效率；提出面向部署的成本目标函数，完整刻画LLM推理的计算开销。

Result: 在4个任务和3个LLM上，MO-CAPO在12个案例中的8个上优于NSGA-II基线（噪声R2指标），且往往在更低预算下取得竞争性能；发现的解集覆盖多样的性能-成本权衡。

Conclusion: MO-CAPO能够高效地发现多样化的帕累托前沿近似，使从业者可以根据实际需求从一组具有不同性能-成本权衡的提示中进行选择。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance across a wide range of tasks but are highly sensitive to prompt design, motivating the need for automatic prompt optimization. Existing methods predominantly focus on performance alone, ignoring competing objectives such as inference cost or latency. At the same time, existing work on multi-objective prompt optimization relies on off-the-shelf NSGA-II, ignoring optimization efficiency. As a remedy, we introduce MO-CAPO, a novel multi-objective prompt optimization algorithm that jointly optimizes performance and inference cost while leveraging budget allocation for cost-efficient optimization. We further propose a deployment-oriented cost objective that captures the full computational profile of LLM inference. We evaluate our approach across four tasks and three LLMs and compare it to an NSGA-II-based multi-objective method and state-of-the-art single-objective prompt optimizers. Results show that MO-CAPO consistently identifies strong, robust, and diverse Pareto front approximations while maintaining cost-efficiency. It outperforms the NSGA-II baseline on 8 out of 12 cases in terms of the noisy R2 metric and achieves competitive performances often already at a considerably lower budget. The discovered solution sets span diverse performance-cost trade-offs that are omitted by single-objective optimizers, yet the top-performance candidates remain competitive with single-objective solutions. Additionally, we conduct the first evaluation of multi-objective machine learning experiments that considers generalization and robustness through noisy R2 and approximation gap, enabling a more realistic assessment of solution quality. MO-CAPO enables practitioners to select from an efficiently discovered set of multiple prompts offering different trade-offs between performance and cost.

</details>

Abstract: Large language models inevitably retain sensitive information, defined as inputs that may induce harmful generations, due to training on massive web corpora, raising concerns for privacy and safety. In this work, we reformulate machine unlearning as a precise knowledge re-mapping problem via model editing. We propose ZeroUnlearn, a few-shot unlearning framework. It overwrites sensitive inputs by mapping them to a neutral target state and removing their original representations. ZeroUnlearn enforces representational orthogonality through a multiplicative parameter update with a closed-form solution, enabling efficient and targeted unlearning. We further extend ZeroUnlearn to a gradient-based variant for multi-sample unlearning. Experiments demonstrate that our approach outperforms existing baselines while preserving general model utility. Our code is available at the github: https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/ZeroUnlearn.

However, practical FL deployments often exhibit severe class imbalance and label skew, causing standard aggregation protocols to overfit dominant clients and degrade minority-class performance. We propose a data-free, class-wise contribution estimation and aggregation framework based on logit maximization (CELM) that does not require sharing raw data, client metadata, or auxiliary public datasets. The FL server probes client updates to obtain class-wise evidence scores and assembles a cross-client evidence matrix, which quantifies both per-class competence and class coverage. Using this matrix, we compute contribution weights that upweight clients providing strong, discriminative evidence for underrepresented classes. The resulting aggregation is stable due to simplex constraints and momentum smoothing, and it remains compatible with standard FL training pipelines. ### [38] [A Two-Parameter Weibull Framework for Diagnosing Transformer Weight Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18898)
*Tiexin Ding*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将威布尔分布（极值理论中的两参数族）作为Transformer中逐元素权重幅度分布的诊断框架。通过对12个模型（涵盖7个架构家族）的分析，发现FFN模块和注意力输出投影W_q（传输类）的威布尔形状参数k集中在[1.186, 1.204]的狭窄区间；注意力输入投影W_q、W_k（选择类）偏离威布尔分布；尺度参数λ随训练增长且与sqrt(η/λ_wd)呈强相关。k标识功能类别，λ标识训练进度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有聚合统计指标难以解析Transformer各组件权重的细粒度训练动态，缺乏架构无关的、具有物理意义的诊断框架。

Method: 使用威布尔分布对权重幅度分布进行建模，通过中间80%概率图拟合获得形状参数k和尺度参数λ；对每层每个组件独立拟合，实现逐组件、逐层、逐步的诊断。

Result: （1）传输类（FFN+W_o）的k值高度一致（中位数[1.186,1.204]，跨家族CV=0.51%）；（2）选择类（W_q,W_k）偏离威布尔族，偏离程度受存储方式影响（分离存储 vs GQA vs 合并W_qkv）；（3）λ与训练动态相关，随训练增长且与sqrt(η/λ_wd)呈Pearson r=0.94。

Conclusion: 威布尔分布的两个参数携带正交信息：k标识组件的功能类别（架构无关），λ标识训练进度。该框架为理解Transformer训练动力学提供了可解释的、细粒度的诊断工具。

Abstract: We apply the Weibull distribution -- a two-parameter family from extreme-value theory -- as a diagnostic framework for element-wise weight magnitude distributions in transformers. At initialization, i.i.d. Gaussian weights give |w| ~ HalfNormal, yielding k ~ 1.20 via middle-80% probability-plot fit (the protocol used throughout this work). This anchor makes k a principled, architecture-independent measuring stick for training dynamics; fitting each weight matrix independently at every layer at every checkpoint enables per-component, per-layer, and per-step diagnostics that aggregate statistics cannot resolve.
  Applying this framework to 12 model entries spanning 7 architectural families (Pythia, OLMo-1/2, LLaMA-3, Mistral, Qwen2.5/3) reveals three findings. First, FFN modules and the attention output projection W_o -- the Transmission Class -- fall in a narrow k band: median terminal k in [1.186, 1.204] across 12 entries (cross-family CV = 0.51%), shared across SwiGLU/GeLU activations, Pre-LN/QK-Norm placements, and 70M-14B sizes. Second, the attention input projections W_q, W_k -- the Selection Class -- depart from the Weibull family, with severity shaped by storage: separately-stored Q/K (OLMo-1, OLMo-2) yields k in [0.76, 0.99] (deep); GQA models yield k in [1.10, 1.16] (mild); Pythia's merged W_qkv occupies a transitional zone tracking training budget T/tau monotonically. Third, lambda grows substantially during training and scales with sqrt(eta/lambda_wd) within the Pythia family (Pearson r = 0.94, three Transmission kinds), directionally consistent with Fan et al. (2025). The two parameters carry independent information: k labels the functional class, lambda labels training progress.
  We release npm-weibull-py v0.4 (Python library) and DATABASE_v9_1 at https://github.com/tiexinding/NPM-Weibull-public .

</details>


### [39] [Don't Let Bandit Feedback Pull Continual LLM-Recommender Updates Off Target](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18899)
*Taesan Kim,Hyeongjun Yun,Jaegul Choo,Chung Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对生成式LLM推荐系统持续更新中的曝光偏差和反馈模糊性问题，提出锚定波段策略优化(ABPO)框架，通过在GRPO中引入固定锚点和自归一化逆概率加权、不对称可靠性处理及自我确定性惩罚调节，在多个数据集上取得一致提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM-based推荐系统需要持续的后部署更新，但部署日志仅提供策略形状的上下文赌博机反馈——只有被先前策略曝光的物品才能观察到结果，这导致曝光偏差和部分、不对称的信号（可靠的正反馈和模糊的无响应）。

Method: 提出ABPO框架：(1) 将曝光推荐作为固定锚点插入GRPO轮组，使组内相对归一化校准到先前策略实际曝光的动作；(2) 对两种反馈类型使用自归一化逆概率加权（SNIPS）矫正策略偏差；(3) 不对称处理反馈可靠性：正反馈提供直接认可，无响应可能反映真实不感兴趣或未观察的外部因素；(4) 用模型输出令牌置信度作为自我确定性信号，调节模糊无响应的惩罚。

Result: 在Amazon Reviews和MovieLens的五个领域上，该方法在推荐准确率上实现一致的持续更新增益，且比基线方法更有效地缓解了先前策略导致的曝光偏差。

Conclusion: ABPO框架有效解决了LLM推荐系统持续更新中的曝光偏差和反馈模糊性问题，为策略优化中的偏差矫正和不对称信号处理提供了实用方案。

Abstract: Generative LLM-based recommenders (LLM-Rec) require continual post-deployment updates, yet deployment logs provide only policy-shaped contextual bandit feedback: outcomes are observed solely for items exposed by a prior serving policy, inducing exposure bias and yielding partial, asymmetric signals consisting of relatively reliable positive responses and ambiguous no-responses. We propose an Anchored Bandit Policy Optimization (ABPO) framework for continual LLM-Rec updates that combines group-relative policy optimization (GRPO) with explicit treatment of exposure bias and feedback ambiguity. Specifically, we insert the exposed recommendation as a logged anchor into each GRPO rollout group, so that group-relative normalization is calibrated against the action actually exposed by the prior policy rather than against newly sampled rollouts alone. Because both positive- and no-responses are observed only through prior-policy exposure, we apply self-normalized inverse propensity scoring to the fixed anchor for both feedback types to correct for policy mismatch. At the same time, we treat the two feedback types asymmetrically in reliability: positive responses provide relatively direct endorsement signals, whereas no-responses remain ambiguous because they may reflect either true disinterest or unobserved external factors. To avoid overly aggressive updates from ambiguous no-responses, we temper their penalties with self-certainty, using the model's output-token confidence as a verifier-free reliability signal. Across five domains from Amazon Reviews and MovieLens, our method yields consistent post-update gains in recommendation accuracy while mitigating prior-policy-induced exposure bias more effectively than prior baselines.

</details>

*Abderrahim Bendahi,Adrien Fradin,Johan Peralez,Julie Digne,Madiha Nadri*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管DeepONet和FNO等神经算子方法在求解PDE方面取得了成功，但连续理论与离散数值实现之间精确的理论联系尚未建立，特别是连续形式与离散数值稳定性之间的关系尚未被充分探索。

Abstract: Neural operators have emerged as a powerful, discretization-invariant framework for solving partial differential equations (PDEs). Although established approaches like the Deep Operator Network (DeepONet) have successfully achieved universal approximation for operators, and architectures such as Fourier Neural Operators (FNOs) have shown algebraic convergence rates, a precise theoretical connection between the continuous theory and its discrete numerical implementation remains a challenge. Specifically, the relationship between the continuous formulation and the discrete numerical stability has yet to be fully explored. In this paper, we address this gap by establishing theoretical guarantees for the discretization error and stability of neural operator approximation schemes. We prove analytical bounds that link solution regularity to input discretization, providing a formal quantification of neural operator accuracy under real-world numerical constraints. We derive these bounds to the specific cases of State Space Model-based Neural Operators (SS-NOs) and FNOs, thus providing a new discretization error theorem for these models. Additionally, through an input-to-state stability (ISS) analysis, we formally assess the impact of discretization on the stability of SS-NOs results obtained in the continuous domain. Our empirical experiments on 1D and 2D benchmarks validate our theoretical bounds and show the robustness of SS-NOs under varying resolutions.

### [41] [Metric-Gradient Projection for Stable Multi-Agent Policy Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18809)
*Zuyuan Zhang,Sizhe Tang,Mahdi Imani,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HPML通过Hodge投影将多智能体系统的联合更新场分解为度量梯度分量（势能部分）和非势能部分，并仅沿梯度分量更新，从而消除循环交互动力学，提升多智能体强化学习的稳定性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体学习中各智能体的策略更新相互耦合，导致联合更新场中存在循环交互分量，使得学习过程缓慢或不稳定。现有方法（正则化、信用分配、共识方法）通过局部或算法修改来稳定MARL，但缺乏从全局几何视角处理更新场中非势能成分的通用框架。

Method: 将多智能体联合更新场视为L²向量场空间中的元素，通过Hodge分解投影到最近的度量梯度势流上。该投影变分地定义，由Poisson型方程刻画，并通过基于图的和摊销的神经实现从样本中恢复投影方向。

Result: 投影动力学具有Lyapunov势函数，并给出带有显式非势能项的均衡间隙界。控制实验验证了几何机制的有效性，CTDE基准测试表明HPML作为插件式投影层可提升稳定性和归一化回报。

Conclusion: HPML从全局几何视角提供了一种与现有MARL方法互补的稳定化工具，通过移除更新场中的循环分量来加速收敛并提升稳定性。

Abstract: General-sum multi-agent learning is often governed by a stacked update field in which each agent's policy update changes the optimization landscape faced by the others. This coupling can entangle an integrable component of collective improvement with cyclic interaction dynamics, leading to slow or unstable multi-agent learning. Existing approaches, such as regularization, credit assignment, and consensus methods, stabilize MARL through local or algorithmic modifications; HPML complements them by projecting the joint update field onto a metric-gradient component. We introduce \textbf{HPML} (\textbf{H}odge-\textbf{P}rojected \textbf{M}ulti-agent \textbf{L}earning), which views the joint update field of a multi-agent system as an element of an $L^2$ space of vector fields and computes a Hodge-type projection onto the closest metric-gradient potential flow. HPML follows the projected component as the update direction, yielding the closest metric-gradient field under the chosen metric and sampling measure. The projection is defined variationally, characterized by a Poisson-type equation, and implemented through graph-based and amortized neural realizations that recover projected directions from samples. We show that the projected dynamics admit a Lyapunov potential and yield equilibrium-gap bounds with an explicit additive non-potentiality term. Controlled experiments validate the geometric mechanism, and CTDE benchmarks show improved stability and normalized return when HPML is used as a plug-in projection layer in MARL pipelines.

</details>


### [42] [Descriptive versus Regulatory Uncertainty in Bounded Predictive Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18909)
*Ahmed Gamal Eldin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明当前Transformer架构在推理时仅具有描述性不确定性（descriptive uncertainty），而非调节性不确定性（regulatory uncertainty），即不确定性不参与动态调控系统行为。通过理论证明（Landauer原理）和三个规模（3B/8B/70B）模型的实验验证，发现token级香农熵在不同任务间统计不变（0.011-0.028 nats差异），而准确率在0%-100%间变化，熵与准确率正交，且该解耦现象具有尺度不变性。真正 epistemic grounding 需要热力学基底状态与信息处理成本的物理耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究尚未明确不确定性是否参与调控系统未来行为的动力学过程，还是仅描述输出分布而不产生实质性影响。本文旨在区分这两种不确定性并检验当前主流架构的能力边界。

Method: 首先从理论上区分为描述性不确定性（不递归调节策略）与调节性不确定性（直接进入优化景观驱动持续适应性重构），基于Landauer原理证明在解耦系统中幻觉与正确推导消耗相同能量。然后在3B/8B/70B三个本地部署的语言模型上，对模式检索、因果算子应用、分布外因果泛化三类任务进行token级香农熵测量与准确率对比。

Result: 三类模型在所有任务上熵几乎不变（0.011-0.028 nats波动，p>=0.568），而准确率在0%-100%间大幅变化。熵与准确率完全正交。该解耦现象具有尺度不变性：更大模型准确率更高，但熵平坦性完全相同。

Conclusion: 当前Transformer架构存在结构性能力缺陷，无法通过增加参数或训练数据解决。真正意义上的认知接地（epistemic grounding）需要信息处理成本与热力学基底状态之间存在物理耦合。

Abstract: Any system that models the world under finite representational capacity must compress; any compression entails a prior; and the prior is the system's bias. What has not been established is whether uncertainty participates in the dynamics governing future behavior, or merely describes the output distribution without consequence. We introduce a structural distinction between descriptive uncertainty, which does not recursively modulate the system's policy, and regulatory uncertainty, which directly enters the optimization landscape and drives persistent adaptive restructuring. We prove formally that current transformer architectures are confined to descriptive uncertainty at inference. We ground this in thermodynamics via Landauer's principle: for uncertainty to be regulatory, epistemic error must cost real energy; in a decoupled system, hallucinations and correct derivations dissipate identical energy. We test this empirically across three locally-deployed language models (3B, 8B, 70B parameters). Token-level Shannon entropy is statistically invariant across tasks spanning pattern retrieval, causal operator application, and out-of-distribution causal generalization in all three models (all pairwise p >= 0.568; within-model ranges 0.011-0.028 nats), while task accuracy varies substantially across the same conditions (0%-100%). Entropy and accuracy are orthogonal. The decoupling is scale-invariant: larger models achieve higher accuracy but identical entropy flatness. This structural incapacity is not resolvable by additional parameters or training data. Genuine epistemic grounding requires physical coupling between thermodynamic substrate state and information processing cost.

</details>
